  <script>
    if (window.L) {
      L.webview.on("VISIBLE", function() {
        L.trackOnce({
          eventType: "PAGE_1"
        });
        setTimeout(function() {
          L.trackOnce({
            eventType: "AD_VIEWABLE"
          });
        }, 1000);
      });
      L.webview.on("CLOSED", function() {

      });
      L.webview.on("HIDDEN", function() {

      });

      window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        if (document.getElementById("loopme-base_1").hasAttribute("data-loopme-loading-page")) {
          document.getElementById("LM_loading_page").addEventListener("click", function() {

          });
        }

        var currentPos = document.getElementById('skeleton').style.backgroundPositionX;

      });
      window.addEventListener("load", function() {
        if (document.getElementById("loopme-base_1").hasAttribute("data-loopme-loading-page")) {
          document.getElementById("LM_loading_page").addEventListener("click", function() {

          });
        }
      });
      if (L.isIOS) {
        window.addEventListener("orientationchange", function() {
          var customEventName = document.querySelector("#loopme-base_1").dataset.customEventName || "";
          if (Math.abs(window.orientation) === 90) {
            // Landscape
            if (isiPad) {

              document.getElementById("landscape").style.display = "block";
            }
            if (L.webview.state == 'VISIBLE') {
              L.track({
                eventType: "INTERACTION",
                customEventName: customEventName + "&mode=SCREEN_ROTATED_L"
              });
            }

          } else {
            // Portrait
            document.getElementById("landscape").style.display = "none";


          }
        })
      };

    }
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript" id="gwd-init-code">
    (function() {
      var gwdAd = document.getElementById('gwd-ad');
      /**
       * Handles the DOMContentLoaded event. The DOMContentLoaded event is
       * fired when the document has been completely loaded and parsed.
       */
      function handleDomContentLoaded(event) {
          // This is a good place to show a loading or branding image while
          // the ad loads.
          //gamma 
          gwd.swipeArea = document.getElementById('gwd-gesture_1');
          gwd.iOSVersion = parseFloat(
            ('' + (/CPU.*OS ([0-9_]{1,5})|(CPU like).*AppleWebKit.*Mobile/i.exec(navigator.userAgent) || [0, ''])[1]).replace('undefined', '3_2').replace('_', '.').replace('_', '')) || false;
          if (L.isIOS && L.isIFrame) {
            if (gwd.iOSVersion >= 10 && gwd.iOSVersion !== false) {
              gwd.swipeArea.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
              window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
                if (event.data.eventData.gamma === 'undefined' || event.data.eventData.gamma == null) {
                  gwd.swipeArea.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                  gyro(event.data.eventData.gamma, 4, false);
                };
              });
            };
          } else {
            window.addEventListener('deviceorientation', function(event) {
              if (event.gamma === 'undefined' || event.gamma == null) {
                gwd.swipeArea.style.display = 'block';
              } else {
                gyro(event.gamma, 4, false);
              };
            });
          };
          gwd.swipeArea.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
            var touchobj = e.changedTouches[0] // reference first touch point (ie: first finger)
            startx = parseInt(touchobj.clientX) // get x position of touch point relative to left edge of browser
            e.preventDefault();
          }, false);
          gwd.swipeArea.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
            var touchobj = e.changedTouches[0] // reference first touch point for this event
            var dist = parseInt(touchobj.clientX) - startx
            gyro(dist, 6, true);
            e.preventDefault();
          }, false);
        }
        /**
         * Handles the WebComponentsReady event. This event is fired when all
         * custom elements have been registered and upgraded.
         */

      function handleWebComponentsReady(event) {
          // Start the Ad lifecycle.
          setTimeout(function() {
            gwdAd.initAd();
          }, 0);
          gwd.toggleLandscapeImage = function(event) {
            customEventName = document.querySelector("#loopme-base_1").dataset.customEventName || "";
            console.log(document.querySelector("#loopme-base_1").dataset.customEventName);
            if (window.innerWidth > window.innerHeight) { //landscape
              document.getElementById("landscape").style.display = "block";
            };
            //ipad webfullscreen hack
            if (L.isIFrame && isiPad) {
              if (Math.abs(window.orientation) === 90) {
                // Landscape
                document.getElementById("landscape").style.display = "block";
              }
            }
          };
        }
        /**
         * Handles the event that is dispatched after the Ad has been
         * initialized and before the default page of the Ad is shown.
         */

      function handleAdInitialized(event) {
        // This marks the end of the polite load phase of the Ad. If a
        // loading image was shown to the user, this is a good place to
        // remove it.
      }
      window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', handleDomContentLoaded, false);
      window.addEventListener('WebComponentsReady', handleWebComponentsReady, false);
      window.addEventListener('adinitialized', handleAdInitialized, false);
    })();
  </script>


</body></html>
